After the Capture of Honghu, the Hunan and Hubei Armies Surrounded and Suppressed the Remaining Bandits of He Long and Kuang Jis勋 73

Xiao Zhichu opened up Western Hubei after clearing Northern Hubei.

Hankou Correspondence: Honghu, which had been occupied by the Communists for two years, was subjected to a general offensive by the entire 10th Army starting on New Year's Day. After repeated breakthroughs of key passes, the bandit forces could not withstand the attack and began to collapse on the 10th. By the 18th, the bandits had been completely routed, and the 10th Army troops completely recovered Honghu the following day. Initially, the bandits occupied Honghu, building fortifications in Sanguandian and Bailuhu, attempting to resist stubbornly. Furthermore, the bandit leaders He Long and Kuang Jixun were fleeing from Hunan to Hubei. Near Shishou, Diaoxian, and Ouchi, there were large numbers of bandits stationed. The bandits affiliated with He Long and Kuang, such as Xun Zaiyang's group, led several thousand people, occupying Liujiachang, Xizhai, Jieheshi, Yanglinshi, Shadaoguan, Mijitai, Yuanshi, and Gongan County, causing great chaos. Therefore, the bandits in Honghu were completely unprepared. As the bandits He Long and Kuang fled to Hubei territory, the Hunan army's Li Jue unit and Dai Huiyuan's brigade immediately pursued and attacked. The 48th Division and the New 10th Division also deployed troops to intercept them. Attacked from both sides, He Long and Kuang were unable to connect with Honghu. The 48th Division then used the strength of six brigades to launch a general offensive against Honghu. Xu Jiwu's brigade first captured Sanguandian, Bailuhu, and other places. Zhang Zhenhan, Han Changjun, Xu Dezhuo, Liu Peixu, Rong Jingfang, and other brigades continued to advance. The bandits, without outside aid and having lost all the strategic points, had no fighting spirit. It is estimated that two to three thousand people were killed by the army, over one thousand were captured, over one thousand killed each other, and over one thousand fled. Therefore, the Communist Party's stronghold in Hubei, from which they issued orders, was captured by the government army. After Xu's brigade and others recovered Honghu, they ordered the burning of the false party headquarters, government, and reactionary propaganda. They immediately telegraphed Xu Yuanquan, the commander-in-chief of the 16th Route Army, for instructions. After receiving the telegram, Xu immediately sent a reply commending them and instructing them on three post-war measures: (1) In the cleared areas, a portion of the army should be responsible for handling the clear-up work together with the county magistrate and local mass organizations. (2) A portion of the army should be dispatched to pursue and suppress the bandits who fled from Honghu day and night to eliminate the roots. (3) The areas near Honghu that are still occupied by the bandits must be wiped out within a time limit. After receiving the order, Xu and other brigade commanders are actively proceeding in different directions. The pursuit troops have reached Yuyangguan, Liujiachang, Xizhai, and other places, and have contacted Dai Huiyuan and Zhou Xieqing and Deng Nanxun's units of the Hunan army at Shimen and Daquanzhi. They will launch a general offensive against He Long and Kuang's bandit forces. It is heard that He Long and Kuang's remaining bandits, after being severely attacked by the Hunan and Hubei armies, hope to flee back to Shihe's old nest. Guo Yun's unit of the Sichuan army rushed to Songzi, Yidu, and Zhijiang to block them. They defeated the majority of the bandits at Liujiachang, and they fled back to Sangzhi and Dayong. Guo ordered the Su militia to defend Wufeng County, and the Yang militia to station in Changyang and Yidu, and contacted Li Xiang's brigade to prevent them from fleeing back to Hubei territory. Liu Xiang, the commander-in-chief of the 7th Route Army, also sent Luo Qijiang's unit to garrison the border between Sichuan and Hubei to prevent them from fleeing to Sichuan. The large armies of each province have completed their communication and surrounded He Long and Kuang's two units. It is estimated that it can be resolved in a few days. As for Chu's unit of the 44th Division, which was originally designated to garrison Western Hubei, was ordered to suppress the bandits because of the rampant communist bandits in Northern Hubei. Now it has cleared up the remaining bandits in the Huang'an area. It is heard that it will still open up Western Hubei to garrison, and search and suppress the remaining bandits with Xu Yuanquan's 48th Division. (January 21st)

The 19th Route Army Sends Reinforcements to Jiangxi 74

Departing from the 17th, they will travel in four batches to Shaozhou and then transfer to Dayu. The front has dispatched Ma's brigade and Deng's regiment south to Dayu to meet them. Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the two divisions of the 19th Route Army, led by Cai Tingkai and Dai Ji, arrived in Xingguo and Yudu in Jiangxi, they are about to launch a large-scale encirclement of the communist bandits in western Jiangxi. It will be difficult to proceed in the future without substantially strengthening their strength and replenishing ammunition. Therefore, after Cai's division arrived in Ganzhou and Yudu, they sent troops to open the road from Ganzhou to Dayu on the Guangdong border in preparation for receiving supplies. The senior officers of the 19th Route Army, such as Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai, made various replenishment plans in Guangzhou. For the 60th Division, there are two special service battalions and five new soldier training teams, totaling more than 1,800 people, preparing to depart in Guangdong. For the 61st Division, there are three special service battalions and five new soldier training teams. The new soldiers in each team were equipped with full arms on the 16th. The Yuehan Railway Bureau was also ordered to prepare vehicles daily, sufficient to transport a regiment of soldiers, stationed at the Huangsha Railway Station awaiting orders. On the 17th, the first batch of troops took a special train north at noon, including four companies of the Second Independent Battalion of the 61st Division, led by Zhong Ding, about 600 people, hundreds of boxes of rifle ammunition, and a company of logistical troops of the 60th Division, more than 200 new soldiers, led by Pang Cheng, the commander of the 13th Regiment of the 7th Brigade of the 61st Division, on a special train of 15 vehicles. They arrived in Shaoguan on the evening of the 17th. On the 18th, a second batch of troops departed. It was found to be about 600 people from the Third Independent Battalion of the 61st Division and about 600 people from the First Independent Battalion of the 60th Division, totaling 1,200 people, led by Battalion Commander Luo Zaoshi, who arrived in Shaozhou at about 4 pm on the 18th. As for the third batch, it included the Special Service Battalion of the 9th Brigade of the 61st Division, led by Zhang Yan, the commander of the 9th Brigade, accompanied by Luo Ding, the director of the new army training, who took a train north on the 19th. Chen Xinlu, the chief of staff of the 60th Division, Ye Shaoquan, the director of the business office, Chen Quan, the chief of the military law office, and dozens of staff members of the two divisions stationed in the Jinghan area, and about 600 people from the Second Special Service Battalion of the 60th Division, led by Cai Tingkai, the commander of the 60th Division, are scheduled to take a train to Shaozhou on the 20th. After each batch of troops arrived in Shaoguan, they did not stay and immediately advanced to Nanxiong and concentrated in Dayu, waiting for the 19th Route Army in Ganzhou to send a team to connect with them. According to the front-line telegram, the 60th Division and the 61st Division sent out various battalions of replenishment regiments and Deng Zhicai's regiment on the 15th to move from Ganzhou south to meet them. Once Deng's regiment arrives in Dayu, the new recruits and officers from Guangdong who arrive in Nanxiong will meet and go to Ganzhou. At the same time, in order to ensure the plan, the 19th Route Army dispatched Ma Kun's brigade south to clear up the remaining bandits between Nan'an and Dayu, and dispatched teams to defend the area, consolidating the border defense between Guangdong and Jiangxi. It is heard that the reinforcements sent from Guangdong to Jiangxi this time brought 400,000 yuan in silver for the two divisions, 20,000 sets of cotton clothes, and 600 boxes of ammunition, which will be sent to Xingguo and distributed to the soldiers at the front. The Public Security Bureau here has hired 300 coolies to escort the military supplies along the way, and they are expected to arrive at their destination around the 25th or 26th. (January 18th)

Ge Guangting Arrives in Qingdao to Take Office 76

Qingdao Correspondence: The newly appointed Director of the Jiaoji Railway, Ge Guangting, arrived in Qingdao by the No. 2 train at 9:00 AM today (the 20th). The various committee members and the heads of each department of the railway, as well as representatives from various agencies, went to the station to welcome him. He said that this time he came to Qingdao without a clear understanding of the internal situation and affairs of the Jiaoji Railway. He added that it is not convenient to announce the railway's ongoing plans and rectification policies until he has consulted with the committee members. (January 20th)

The Tragic Decline of Changchun's Commerce 77

Affected as Severely as the Provincial Capital by the Plummeting Value of Paper Money

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Cables the Provincial Government Appealing for Relief

Changchun Correspondence: Changchun, a vital town in the Northeast and the meeting point of the three railways – the Chinese Eastern, South Manchurian, and Jichang – boasts convenient transportation and was renowned for its thriving commerce. Since the surge in the price of gold, it has suffered significant losses. Recently, the official notes of Jilin Province, the main currency, have plummeted in value, inflicting even more severe wounds. The market is in turmoil, making it almost impossible to sustain. The Manchurian Railway-occupied areas in Toutaogou are becoming commercial wastelands, and the situation is even worse in the commercial districts and within the city. The Changchun market is affected by the falling prices of grains and the tightening of credit. Many businesses, both large and small, have been closing down in recent days. Apart from grain merchants and pawnshops, the majority of businesses in the city are retail shops. The price of their goods is mainly based on the Yongheng official notes as the primary currency. However, gold tickets (Japanese gold) are essential for importing foreign goods from places like Osaka, Japan. When purchasing domestic goods from various ports in Tianjin and Shanghai and remitting payments, banknotes (Japanese silver) are used for circulation. In previous years, when new grains came onto the market, grain merchants competed to buy grains and beans, transporting them to Dalian and exchanging them for banknotes to circulate in the market. Therefore, the price of gold and banknotes gradually decreased every winter. However, after the autumn harvest last year, the sale of grains and beans to Dalian was sluggish, preventing grain merchants from purchasing and transporting them, resulting in a lack of banknote sources. Merchants needing gold and banknotes to remit payments had no choice but to buy them, leading to a supply shortage. Consequently, the price of gold and banknotes increased daily, while the official notes depreciated, further tightening the monetary situation. Businesses, with limited capital, found it insufficient for circulation and resorted to borrowing from Chinese and foreign banks at high interest rates. According to investigations, the Bank of Chosen alone loaned approximately three million yuan in gold and banknotes to businesses in the city. State and local banks loaned approximately seven million silver dollars. Currently, the lending institutions, fearing that borrowers will go bankrupt and suffer losses, have stopped lending and are aggressively collecting existing loans. With limited income from sales and external debts being demanded, borrowers have no choice but to declare bankruptcy. Moreover, each loan requires guarantees from two or more guarantors. If the borrower cannot fulfill the repayment obligations, the lenders will inevitably demand payment from the guarantors, who, unable to bear the responsibility, will also have to declare bankruptcy. Therefore, the bankruptcy of one business inevitably leads to the collapse of many others. Recently, as many as fifty-six businesses, large and small, have been affected by this chain reaction. Those that have not yet collapsed are struggling to survive, with no guarantee of making it to the next day. If no measures are taken to provide relief, there is a risk of a complete collapse by the end of the year. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, responsible for protecting businesses, could not remain silent in the face of such a dire situation. Therefore, on the thirteenth of this month, it detailed the actual situation in telegrams to the Jilin Provincial Government and the Agricultural and Mining Bureau, which also oversees industry and commerce, appealing for relief. They requested the Yongheng Official Bank to promptly sell a large amount of banknotes to stabilize the financial situation and pleaded for the ample disbursement of loans to rescue the crisis. It remains to be seen how the authorities will respond. (January 15th)

Anhui Province Reduces Rice Passport Fees and Tax Rates 78

Export Rice Actually Levied at Four Jiao per Stone

Wuhu Correspondence: After the abolition of Likin in Anhui Province, a rice export passport fee was established. The business community, considering it of great importance to the province's commerce, not only telegraphed the National Government and the Provincial Government requesting its abolition, but also dispatched Wu Xingzhou, chairman of the Provincial Federation of Commerce and chairman of the Wuhu General Chamber of Commerce, and Tang Xiaoquan, representatives of the Wuhu Guangdong-Chaozhou and Yanning rice industries, along with nine others, to Anqing to personally present the situation regarding the impact of rice passport fees on commerce to the Provincial Government. They met with Chen Diaoyuan, chairman of the Provincial Government, and Yuan Jiapu, director of the Department of Finance, several times, arguing that after the abolition of Likin in Anhui Province, military and administrative expenses were insufficient by 13.5 million yuan. If no measures were taken to offset this, the Provincial Government would have no choice but to close its doors. All Anhui people had a joint responsibility to maintain the province. The industry had already planned thoroughly, calculating that rice export fees could generate 3.5 million yuan annually, salt surcharge of 2.4 yuan could generate more than 2 million yuan, Weitian increase could generate about 8 million yuan, and business tax could generate about 500,000 yuan. These were all unavoidable measures that had to be implemented. Moreover, for the sake of the province's food supply, rice exports could not be allowed without proper investigation and unlimited exports. The representatives repeatedly requested and negotiated with Director Yuan, who finally agreed to reduce the fee by two jiao, actually levying four jiao per stone for export. The representatives, seeing no other option, returned on the Jiang'an steamer this morning and will convene another meeting to discuss the plan. The 500,000 to 600,000 stones of rice previously concentrated in the port have already been registered for export at the rice passport fee general inspection office because the iron steamships of various groups have been waiting for a long time. Furthermore, rice merchants transporting rice by sail from Lu and He and the six counties of Anqing, as well as Nanling and Yicheng, considered rice passports to be of great importance for transportation within the province. Zhang Jiesan, Li Youren, and Yuan Zhongyi have been selected as representatives to telegraph the Provincial Government, requesting special consideration, and have initiated the organization of the Anhui Province Sail Transport Rice Merchants United Maintenance Business Association, which is scheduled to be established in Wuhu to maintain business operations.

This time, with the nationwide implementation of Likin abolition, the usual customs posts within fifty li were also to be abolished. The Wuhu General Chamber of Commerce previously organized a review committee for the usual customs posts and telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, requesting early abolition to relieve the distress of merchants in Jiangsu. Now, a reply has been received from the Ministry of Finance stating that it must wait until a comprehensive plan is developed before a decision can be made. Therefore, the Chamber held another meeting today and unanimously agreed that the usual customs posts were detrimental to businesses, and unless they were abolished, commerce would never be revived. It was decided to re-telegraph the National Government and the Ministry of Finance, based on the previous request, urging the early abolition of the usual customs posts within fifty li. The Anhui Provincial Federation of Commerce, due to the implementation of business taxes in Jiangsu Province after the Likin abolition, which were ten times higher than the original outline, and with Anhui Province about to implement business taxes, to avoid repeating the same mistake, telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance, requesting that commercial organizations be allowed to participate in the formulation of new taxes. The telegram is as follows: "The new taxes to offset Likin abolition are a special consumption tax in the national treasury and a business tax in the provincial treasury. During the Likin abolition conference, outlines were established to give merchants an opportunity to express their opinions, so as not to repeat the old Likin system, where the tax commissioner had sole authority. Recently, according to newspaper reports, the business tax implemented in Jiangsu Province is ten times higher than the original outline, and it is also heard that the unified tax on yarn factories has been increased to four or five times the original rate. If all provinces follow this new example, the outlines will become mere formalities, and the arbitrary increase of burdens is not the original intention of the state to abolish Likin and eliminate the detrimental policies that harm businesses. It is hoped that you will review the third item of the special consumption tax outline and the fifth article of the business tax outline, and allow commercial organizations to contribute their opinions when formulating new taxes,

Page 10

so as not to lose the original intention of the law and to ensure that the new taxes can be implemented without obstruction. We hope you will consider and adopt this." (January 21st)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 79

Detailed Account of the Robbery and Kidnapping Case in Jiang Village, Punan: Jiang Village in Punan is located six li west of Shanyang, and is six li from remote small towns like Malan Dian and Shanyang Xupu, and just one li from closer ones. The market in the town is declining, but it serves as a hiding place for bandits, so it has been robbed three times in the past two years. It has been learned that at 12:00 pm on the 20th, more than 30 bandits speaking with both local and out-of-town accents suddenly arrived, carrying four quick-firing guns and eight Mauser pistols. They divided into several groups to carry out the robbery. Bandits were stationed in the town to guard and set up sentries. All merchants in the town were robbed, and Xie Zichun, a doctor in the town, and the children of Mr. Tan, the owner of the Yi Ji Nanhua store, were kidnapped, as well as the son of Qi Ziyu and the son of Zhang Heng from the countryside, and a peasant. At dawn, they escorted the six hostages in three boats, carrying the loot and fleeing towards the Dianshan River area. At that time, a police team stationed at Mazha sent out a sentry, who encountered the bandits in Dianshan while patrolling from a neighboring town. They immediately opened fire to suppress them. At the same time, the Xihutang defense corps also heard the gunfire and rushed to the scene, surrounding and attacking the bandits. The fighting was fierce. Many bandits were killed and wounded, and they abandoned the hostages and fled. When the bandits tried to rob the Qi Ziyu family in the countryside, the Qi family had weapons for self-defense and fought the bandits once. At night, when everyone was quiet, the sound of gunfire was heard in the towns, and they prepared for defense. The police team and defense corps came together to attack quickly. The hostages were completely rescued. It was all thanks to the courage of the corps and police.

Police and Corps Capture Bandits and Escort Them to the County for Interrogation: The County Magistrate and the County Clearing Bureau today received four bandits, Wu Yintang, Jiang Awu, Jiang Ali, and Ma Shaoquan, who were escorted to the county by the police team and defense corps stationed in Shanyang. After interrogation, except for Ma Shaoquan, who claimed that he was implicated because his nephew was a thief, Wu Yintang and the other three admitted to robbing Xin Street, Dianshan, and other places, and provided the names of the remaining bandits. They were imprisoned and interrogated, and the bandits were investigated.

Suzhou 80

A Boat Collision Leads to Tragedy: An old woman named Wang from Yuhang Village, Mudang, brought her daughter, Wang Jinfeng, to Suzhou on the Lao Gong Mao Lun ship. When the ship arrived in Suzhou, it collided with a Ningbo boat near the Darihui Bridge. The old woman Wang fell into the river from the cabin. She was rescued by the ship and brought ashore. It was discovered that she had injured her waist. Hua, the accountant of the Lao Gong Mao Lun ship, hired a boat and attached it to the Jicheng steamship to return to Mudang. Unexpectedly, Wang's injuries worsened, and she died of her injuries on the way. After arriving in the town, Wang's body was placed at the Lao Gong Mao Lun port. The local police reported it to the local court, which sent officials to investigate.

Director of Education Accused: He Huanting, a citizen of Suzhou, submitted a report to the Provincial Department of Education last month, accusing Wu Yaozhang, Director of the Wuxian Education Bureau, of laziness and misconduct, requesting that he be dismissed and punished. Director Chen of the Department of Education, after receiving the report, ordered Magistrate Huang to instruct Director Yuan of the Finance Bureau to thoroughly investigate and respond.

Visiting Relatives Ashamed of Getting Dung Poured on Their Face: A local man named Zhou Xingxi recently traveled by boat to Xiangshan to collect rent. Because the ice on Taihu Lake had not melted, he turned to Lili to visit relatives. Unexpectedly, Gu Guitang, a villager, rushed out of the woods and poured dung all over Zhou's face, robbing him of all his 216 yuan in cash, 25 yuan in banknotes, and 12 household deeds. After the incident, Zhou returned to the city yesterday and reported it to the county, requesting an arrest.

Changshu 81

The New Investigating Judge Has Arrived and Assumed Office: It is heard that Judge Gu Yushang has arrived in Changshu on the 20th in exchange for Judge Shi Wending of this county and Judge Gu Yushang of Qidong County. The next day, he went to the county office to handle various cases.

False Alarm in Liantang One Night: The Liantang town area in the Yuanhua district of this county is located on the lake shore, and bandits often take the opportunity to land and rob. At about 12:00 pm on the 20th, several bandit ships were suddenly discovered at Zhangjiaqiao, south of Huadang, carrying about 100 bandits, planning to land and rob. The sentry sent out by the armed unit caught a glimpse of them and immediately summoned the residents to beat the gongs and gather the crowd, while running back to report to the unit for departure. By that time, the bandits had already heard the sound of the gongs and returned to their boats and fled, so they were not robbed.

Wuxi 82

False Refugee Leader Exposed and Arrested: A man named Wang Kexuan from Funing, about 30 years old, dressed luxuriously, passed through Houtuo Town, Taibo City, under the jurisdiction of the county, at 4:00 pm the day before yesterday. He suddenly claimed to Li, the director of the 11th Public Security Bureau in that area, that a large number of Funing refugees were passing through, requesting food and other supplies. Director Li dispatched police officers to inquire and found that no refugees had arrived in the town. Director Li believed that Wang Kexuan was obviously impersonating a refugee leader and extorting food, and immediately ordered the police to detain Wang, who was sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation yesterday.

County Court Officially Established Today: All internal arrangements for the Xiyi County Court have been prepared and officially established today (24th). Yesterday, President Yang and Prosecutor Zhou arrived in Xiyi from Suzhou under appointment, and Yu Jitang and Liang Xuan, the current investigating judges of the county government, have been appointed as candidate judges of the county court by President Lin. Yu has also received an order from the High Court, transferring him to the First Branch of the Jiangsu High Court in Qingjiangpu as a candidate judge of the Wuxian District Court.

Four Robbery Cases Occur in the City and Countryside in One Day: During this winter defense period, robbery cases in the city and countryside are heard every day. Residents generally feel uneasy. Yesterday, news came that four robbery cases occurred in one day. They are recorded as follows: (1) Yao Age, a villager in Shuowang Township, Taibo City, 12th District, went to Mr. Jia's house to collect money. At 1:00 pm, Age was carrying the money home when he encountered a bandit on the south side of Wang Daoren Lane, who blocked his way and robbed Age of all 30 silver dollars he was carrying. Later, Age caught one of the robbers, who was found to be a local villager named Aju. Nearby residents intervened and returned the money. (2) Mr. Zhu, an employee of the Minfeng Silk Factory outside the South Gate, took a streetcar home to his private residence in Taiping Lane outside the Guangfu Gate last night. When he passed Huangtiandang, he was suddenly attacked by three thugs who robbed him of the fur coat he was wearing. Afterwards, the police from the 3rd Public Security Bureau dispatched police officers to arrest the three thugs and bring them to the bureau. However, Mr. Zhu, regardless of the resentment he would incur, requested the bureau to release them, which Director Wang approved. (3) A few bandits also came to the home of Jin Xiaosu, a resident of Chengjiao, outside the North Gate last night and carried out a robbery (some say they entered gently but left violently), resulting in significant losses. (4) Zhai A'er from Xinghua intended to snatch the gold ring worn on the ear of Zou Anong, the daughter of Zou Yongsan, on Xiangshang, 4th District (Kaiyuan Township), yesterday. She was spotted by women Zou Yao, Yuan Li, etc., who immediately twisted Zhai A'er and sent him to the 9th Public Security Bureau for transfer to the General Bureau for interrogation according to law.

Changzhou 83

The Dispute Over the Feast Donation Has Not Yet Been Resolved: The restaurant industry of Wuyi County unanimously opposed the collection of donation money by the Feast Donation Collection Office. From the strike to the resumption of business, representatives of the Tingcai restaurant industry petitioned the party and government organs. The county government ordered the representatives to submit the requested methods for review within three days, but the representatives have not submitted any methods. The Education Bureau has also submitted a petition to the county, accusing the restaurant industry of refusing to pay the donation. On the 22nd, Magistrate Zhang ordered the police to summon six representatives of the restaurant industry, Zhu Jinsheng, Wang Hongsheng, Cai Fusheng, Wang Zirong, Shen Jinsheng, and Li Quanchang, to the county government. Wu, the section chief of the Second Section, spoke to the representatives and ordered them to provide a certificate of compliance with the normal agency collection of donation money, so as to notify the Collection Office to check the accounts and collect donations at each restaurant. The representatives refused. Section Chief Wu then gave a face-to-face instruction. In the evening, Magistrate Zhang, Director Liu of the Public Security Bureau, Director Lin of the Finance Bureau, lawyer Yun Kuiyao of the Chamber of Commerce, etc., met at the Dacheng Hotel to discuss the matter. Magistrate Zhang said that the six representatives were willing to provide a certificate of payment, so they could be released. The restaurant industry still refused. Finally, the leaders of the agencies scheduled a meeting at the county government on the 23rd to discuss and resolve the issue. The six representatives were being held in the Political and Police Waiting for Trial Office.

A Kidnapping Case Occurs in the Fifth District: Xu Denghua, the deputy chief of Wangjia Village, Wanjia Township, Fifth District of Wuyi County, was suddenly attacked by more than 20 bandits, each holding firearms, who searched each room and robbed them of all their clothes, jewelry, and cash. After the robbery, they kidnapped his second son, Xu Xiaowan, and left in the same way, leaving a case demanding 5,000 yuan, to be sent to the Sanhuang Temple for redemption.

A Murder and Robbery Case Occurs in the Eastern Suburbs: Shi Zilin of Shijia Village near Baijia Bridge outside the East Gate of Wuyi County was well-off. He had just finished his son Susheng's wedding on the 13th of the old calendar month. Unexpectedly, at about 10:00 pm on the 20th, more than 10 armed bandits suddenly arrived and first twisted and held Wang Shi Zilin, extorting silver dollars. When he refused, they nailed a file down from Zilin's head, causing his brains to flow out and killing him. Zilin's wife was also severely beaten. They then went to Susheng's new house and wantonly searched for all the cash and clothes, which were looted and taken away. After being injured, the deceased's wife was carried into the city for treatment on the 21st.

Bandits Captured at the Border of Wucheng: At about 10:00 am on the 21st, more than 10 plainclothes policemen from Cheng County arrived at the Xiaohu area on the border of Wujin and Jiangyin County. They were dressed as travelers and sat drinking tea in a teahouse. Soon, Jin, the current chief of the 6th District of Jiangyin, rushed to the scene. The plainclothes police immediately held up firearms and arrested bandits in all directions. Four bandits, including Tan Erda, and two suspects were captured and escorted to Jiangyin. About a li away, a painter bandit stubbornly resisted and was shot and killed by the police, and his body was abandoned on the roadside.

Zhenjiang 84

The Verdict of the Jiangdu Prison Break Case: During the Mid-Autumn Festival of the old calendar last year, 48 detainees escaped from the Jiangdu County Court Detention Center. Later, the High Court commissioned a special investigator to find that the personnel in charge of the detention center were suspected of facilitating the escape. The director of the detention center, Chen Quan, and the director of security, Liu Baichuan, as well as the guards, Jiang Qisheng, Zhou Wenbiao, Lu Dingyuan, Shi Dianwen, Lu Damaozi, Wang Jiren, Tu Guilin, Chen Shulin, Cheng Liuxing, Wei Liben, and Tao Guisen, a total of 13 people, were brought to court for investigation and all detained. Chen Quan and Liu Baichuan were released on bail due to illness. Later, upon the order of the High Court, the case was transferred to the Zhenjiang Court for trial. Chen and Liu were again summoned to court. Chen again used illness as an excuse for not attending. Prosecutor Zhou questioned them one by one and conducted multiple investigations. Shi Dianwen, Jiang Qisheng, and Lu Dingyuan were found to have no criminal suspicion in this case and were released. The remaining nine people, including Liu Baichuan, were suspected of facilitating the escape for eight reasons, and one piece of evidence was used to prosecute the Criminal Court. The case had been openly tried and had been concluded. The verdict was announced at 2:00 pm on the 22nd. Liu Baichuan, Zhou Wenbiao, Chen Shulin, Tu Guilin, Cheng Liuxing, Tao Guisen, Wei Liben, Lu Damaozi, and Wang Jiren were found guilty of facilitating the escape and each sentenced to five years of imprisonment. After the reading of the verdict, they were ordered to be returned to custody. Liu and others claimed that they did not accept the verdict and intended to appeal. Chen Quan is still at large and has been explicitly wanted.

Yangzhou 85

Recent News of the Northern Relocation of the Salt Transport Office: Although the counties and groups in northern Huai have repeatedly appealed for the relocation of the Salt Transport Office to northern Huai, they have never succeeded. Recently, reliable news from Beijing has revealed that the relocation is inevitable. No matter what requests are made, it will be impossible to reverse the decision. However, all taxes will be temporarily collected in Yangzhou. The education, charity, and police surtaxes that have been collected in the past will remain the same. The audit office will not be relocated with the Salt Transport Office. The Huainan Anti-Smuggling Bureau will not be abolished for the time being. The Yangzi Salt Depot will be relocated from Twelve Forts to Yangzhou and its organization will be expanded. The Salt Deputy will be changed from Huabei to Huainan and located in the same city as the Yangzi Salt Depot. Then, the transition from sailing ships to steamship transport will be gradually made. The transition from paying taxes in Yangzhou to collecting them on-site is being made. Although the people of northern Huai do not ask for it, it is actually not easy to change everything at once. It is also heard that the newly appointed Salt Transport Commissioner Wang has assigned four members, Ye, Tan, Wang, and Zhang, to go to Guanyun to take over the Huabei Salt Deputy first. Then, the Huabei Salt Deputy will send personnel to Yangzhou to organize the Huainan Salt Deputy. It is estimated that the procedures for the above-mentioned handover, organization, and relocation will take a month to complete.

Nantong 86

Establishment of the Local Pacification Office: The military, political, and police agencies of Tong County have established a local pacification office to eliminate the remaining bandits and communists in the territory. They have reported it to the Provincial Pacification Supervisor for record. Shi Dexue has been appointed as the director, and Zhang Dong and Wang Dechang have been appointed as the deputy directors.

Lusi Pirates Fight Again: On the 22nd, a large group of pirates in the Third Jia Town of Lusi had another internal conflict, resulting in fighting on the sea. The pirate leader, Pan Kaiwu, was confirmed to have been shot and killed, and several pirate ships were sunk. The pirates are in disarray. The State Army Shi Group has rushed to suppress them.

Jisheng Case Excessively Collected Beach Fields Confiscated: The excess collection of 1,100 mu of beach fields in the sixth and seventh dikes in the Liu Haisha Jisheng case has been resolved by the provincial government. The price of each mu will be 60 yuan and reported to the Education Bureau for receipt. The field price will be transferred to the national treasury.

Lost Weapons Police Captain Imprisoned: Xu Guanxiong, the captain of the county police squad, lost more than 100 rifles to bandits during the suppression of bandits in Dongxiang. He was dismissed from his post and investigated by the county government. Later, he was ordered to be interrogated by the Provincial Security Office. He has been sent back and imprisoned in the Fourth Prison for two years according to the judgment.

Notification of Coastal Anti-Banditry Martial Law: A notification has been issued to all counties along the coast that the military and police are suppressing sea bandits. All areas fear that bandits will cause trouble and temporary martial law has been imposed. County Magistrate Tan of Changshu has come to Tong to discuss coastal defense and join the Tonghai Qiji joint defense zone.

Pinghu District Chief Detained in the Province: Zhang Kui, the district chief of Pinghu, has been detained in the province by the Department of Civil Affairs due to the Wu Yang bandit case in the district. The county government has been ordered to examine the files for review.

Pinghu 87

Bandit Harassment Strikes Again: Two Incidents in Pinghu's Countryside. At Qianmei Village's Juloutang in Pinghu, on the 21st, around 8 PM, four bandit boats arrived, towed by a small steamer. Over 30 bandits, armed with rapid-fire guns and Mauser pistols, stormed into the homes of Fan Awu and Fan Sanhe, looting rice and clothing worth about 500 yuan, and injuring Awu's son, Xiaoliu. Also, in Xincang South Xiele Bridge in the eastern countryside, Tang Erdi, a musician, was extorted for 3,000 yuan by the bandit Liu Dexing earlier in the month. Tang's family fled to avoid payment, angering the bandits. On the 21st, several bandits went to Tang's house, carrying rice straw into the house and setting it on fire. The ancestral hall was already ablaze, threatening the entire house. Neighbors pleaded with the bandits repeatedly, and the fire was finally extinguished. However, the bandits threatened to return and burn the house again if Tang did not quickly pay the money.

Commander Shen Narrowly Escapes Bandit Capture: Commander Shen of the 7th Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Force went to Xincang Town in eastern Pinghu on the 20th to inspect defenses and gathered soldiers of the 11th Company stationed there for a briefing. On the 21st, he took a small steamer he had procured back to Pinghu, escorted by a platoon of soldiers from the 11th Company. Upon reaching Guangchen Town, Shen instructed the escorting soldiers to return to Xincang. He continued in the steamer with a Mr. He, a staff member from the regimental headquarters, and several soldiers. Near Banlu Bridge, several bandit boats suddenly blocked their path, and bandits boarded Shen's steamer. One soldier was tied up, and another was knocked into the water. Commander Shen's insignia was torn off by the bandits. Fortunately, the bandits could not read, so Shen claimed to be a salt affairs official, narrowly escaping harm. The bandits severely beat Shen and Mr. He before releasing them, stealing over 80 yuan in cash that Shen had with him. A Pinghu water police officer, acting as Shen's guide, jumped into the river and swam away to escape. Mr. He's injuries were serious, while Shen's were lighter. On the 22nd, they arrived in Pinghu together to see a doctor at the hospital, and Shen returned to Hangzhou in the afternoon. The water police and security forces dispatched troops and police to Banlu Bridge to search for the bandits, but they had already fled.

Huzhou 88

Military and Bandits Exchange Fire in Western Suburbs: The Security 4th Company belonging to Huzhou, led by Commander Zhang Zheng Bingyi; the Detective Squad, led by Zhang; the defense corps from places like Xucang Bridge and the port; as well as the Hongxing Bridge water police, jointly suppressed bandits in the Taiping Bridge area of Changxing County. On the 20th of this month, around 4 AM, they suddenly encountered a large band of bandits and immediately opened fire. After about an hour of fighting, the bandits were overwhelmed and fled in all directions. Two bandits were killed on the spot, and Chen Xingde, Wan Baoan, Wang Kaizhou, Hu Qihe, Wang Yushan, and five others were captured alive. Four Mauser rifles and one Murata rifle were seized. It is said that these firearms all had serial numbers and were weapons seized from the Xiaang water police.

Over 300 Refugees Arrive in Zhili Town: Yesterday, the 21st, around 8 PM, over 300 refugees suddenly arrived in Zhili Town outside the North Gate of this city. They were on 31 boats of various sizes, moored in the town's canal, causing panic among all the townspeople. The town's public security bureau, with its limited police force, was at a loss and urgently telegraphed the Wuxing County Government in this city. The county government, upon receiving the telegram, immediately ordered the county police force to dispatch over 30 police officers to maintain order.

Jiaxing 89

Qixing Bridge Train Station to be Constructed: The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration has designed and is building a train station at Qixing Bridge between Jiaxing and Jiashan to facilitate travel. It has been learned that the administration ordered dozens of workers to drive stakes, erect poles, and fill earthwork there the day before yesterday, planning to use approximately fifty mu of land in total. However, local residents, believing that the land is privately owned and has not been purchased, protested the excavation, causing considerable disturbance. Mr. Xie, a village committee member, intervened to mediate, instructing the workers to temporarily halt the destruction of fields, so that the land could be priced and paid for later. He also came to the city to report to the district office, accompanied by District Chief Mei, to meet with the Jiaxing stationmaster, explain everything, and request that the administration be telegraphed for further instructions.

Neighborhood Head Shot Dead by Bandits in Dongsheli: The home of Zhou Ajin, a resident of Dongsheli, which is under the jurisdiction of Changfengli in Dongzhakou, Jiaxing First District, was robbed the night before last. Xu Xiaoer, the neighborhood head, heard the commotion and went outside to shout for help but was shot in a vital area by the thieves and died instantly. At the same time, several residents, including Ma Yongtao, were also shot and injured by the bandits.

Xiaoshan 90

Autonomous Household Donations to be Audited First: The Xiaoshan district and township offices are now preparing to be formally established. The county government previously ordered villages and neighborhoods to collect autonomous household donations, but most of the money was pocketed by the village and neighborhood heads. Recently, Special Commissioner Du dispatched by the County Magistrate has been assigned to audit the collection of autonomous household donations in various districts, starting with the 18th and 19th years' donations that have already been collected. For the 20th year, the county will jointly dispatch staff with the township offices to compile and investigate before collecting donations again.

Night Boat Robbed Twice: On the 21st at night, a cargo boat sailing from Linpu to Shaocheng on the Xiaoxi River, which borders Shaoxing and Xiaoshan, was stopped and robbed by two bandit boats near Mashe Bridge. Cloth and silver dollars totaling over 200 yuan were stolen, and a boat hand named Asheng was slashed in the leg. Unexpectedly, when the boat reached Yangfan Bridge, it was stopped by another bandit boat and searched for a second time. Crude goods worth over 100 yuan were lost. The bandits fled as dawn approached.

Forced Collection of Mu Tax to be Investigated and Strictly Punished: Zhang Quanxin and others, cadres of the Agricultural Association outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan, were privately collecting mu tax at a rate of 3.5 jiao per mu, leading to accusations from farmers. The county dispatched personnel to investigate and confirmed the facts. Police have already been dispatched to arrest them. Also, the Nongxie Associations in Dongcao and Tongji, and other townships extorted three sheng of rice per mu as membership fees, which also led to accusations from the public.

Anqing 91

Handling of the Party Case at Southeast Middle School: The Anqing Southeast Private Middle School was recently discovered by the provincial authorities to have reactionary elements. The Provincial Public Security Bureau was ordered to arrest the school's principal, Fang Botang, and the director of studies, Zhang Zishi, and hand them over to the Provisional Military Tribunal for trial. The Provincial Government Standing Committee decided on the 20th to: 1. Dissolve Southeast School; 2. Sentence Fang Botang to one year of imprisonment under Article 6 of the Provisional Regulations for the Punishment of Counter-Revolutionaries. The school, originally located in the old provincial yamen, was approved by the Department of Education and the Provincial Government to be allocated as the site for the Training Institute for Educational Administrative Personnel.

Never Return Ni's Ill-Gotten Gains: Groups such as the Fuyang County Party Committee and the Education Bureau telegraphed the Provincial Government to inquire about the request by Ni Sichong's sons and nephews for the return of their ill-gotten gains. The Provincial Government replied yesterday, stating that Ni's property had already been disposed of, and the government had never mentioned returning it. This is a special reply.

Educational News

Important News

Jiangsu Education Department Inspection Meeting 92

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department Inspection Meeting was held at 2 PM on January 21st. Attendees included Chen Hexian, Yang Naikang, Xiang Shaoxuan, Zhou Yuxin, Xiang Zitan, Cao Shutian, Li Jiahan, Yu Qingtang, and Liu Shaozhen (as a representative). Hou Bingji and Huang Shaohong were absent due to illness. The meeting was chaired by Department Head Chen Hexian, with Huang Shaohong as the recorder. The chair respectfully read Premier Sun Yat-sen's last testament.

Items for Discussion: 1. Whether district inspectors assigned to various counties but not yet inspecting should be assigned a date for inspection. Resolution: The inspection departure date is set for February 20th, the inspection completion date is set for the end of March, and the report submission date is set for the end of April. 2. How should the eleven counties not yet assigned for inspection be divided? Resolution: (1) The Department will first issue orders to the counties to prepare for the inspectors' visits; (2) The distribution of responsibilities for each county will be decided by the inspectors based on local conditions. Inspector Cao will be responsible for Suining and Suqian Counties; Inspector Xiang will be responsible for Tongshan and Pi Counties; Inspector Yi will be responsible for Donghai, Guanyun, and Gan Yu Counties; Inspector Zhou will be responsible for Feng County, Pei County, Xiao County, Dangshan and other counties. 3. Whether the 19th year's educational expenditures in each county were indeed implemented in accordance with the approved budget. 4. For counties with accumulated educational expense deficits, the inspectors should be requested to consult with the county government and convene the finance and education bureaus to jointly discuss a clearing method in accordance with the Department's regulations. 5. Whether the economic audit committees of educational institutions in each county have been organized and whether monthly income and expenditures have been submitted to the full committee for review. In addition to the Department revising the regulations and issuing separate orders for compliance, the inspectors should pay attention to the matter. The above three items were discussed together. Resolution: Each inspector should conduct a strict investigation and urge implementation. For those counties under inspection that have not yet established economic audit committees and debt clearing committees, the fourth section should create a list and submit it to each inspector, and the Department should order each county to comply. 6. Please inspect the actual work status of local educational instructors from the provincial elementary schools at any time. 7. Please assess whether each county education bureau has submitted and approved the 19th year's administrative plan for implementation. The above two items were discussed together. Resolution: The inspectors should assess and urge compliance during their visits to the counties, ensuring thorough compliance. 8. Is there a need to implement the high school consolidation plan? 9. Should the junior high school reform focus on cultivating low-level agricultural and industrial improvement talents? 10. Should the final year of higher elementary school emphasize vocational skills? The above three items were discussed together. Resolution: A discussion of the joint plans will occur after the inspectors have completed their inspections and submitted their overall reports. 11. Many internal staff members of the county education bureaus hold more than two positions (such as inspectors doubling as section chiefs, or education committee members doubling as section members). Should this be observed at any time to avoid negligence? Resolution: The Department will draft remedies and submit them to the Provincial Government for approval and circulation for compliance. 12. How should the basic educational ideology of principals and teachers be assessed to determine its purity? 13. How should elementary school teachers' research on multi-grade teaching methods and self-cultivation methods be enriched? 14. All private secondary schools in each county, whether registered or unregistered, should be inspected strictly. 15. Should elementary schools with few students that insist on offering complete elementary education be strictly banned, given that only a few students are in the fifth and sixth grades, resulting in significant expenses? The above four items were discussed together. Resolution: Regarding correcting ideological aspects, each inspector should conduct a strict assessment and urge each school to use textbooks that have been reviewed. If there are still unsatisfactory textbooks, they should be submitted to the Ministry of Education for correction. Unreviewed textbooks and those with impure ideologies should not be used under any circumstances. As for those who do not understand teaching methods and private schools that are not registered, as well as those that cannot operate complete elementary schools, they should be assessed, urged, and banned at any time. 16. Printing inspection reports is proposed to be published in four phases. Resolution: (1) The first and second phases should be published first, and the third and fourth phases should be printed after the inspection is completed, along with an overall conclusion. (2) The editorial style of the publications should be handled by Hou and the book club in consultation with the inspectors.

New Officials Appointed to Zhejiang Education Department 93

The Zhejiang Education Department recently appointed two secretaries, Shen Fuzhai (originally from Zhejiang, currently in Sichuan, professor at National Jinan University) and Chen Jingyang (originally from Zhejiang, currently in Beiping, formerly a professor at National Jinan University); one section chief (First Section), Xiong Wenmin (from Jiangxi); two clerks, Zhang Yunming and Zuo Jiandong; and two scribes, Wang Yijie and Zheng Lisheng. All of the above officials have been appointed to fill vacancies. Zheng Hechun, the original chief of the First Section, has been appointed as the Magistrate of Jingning County by the Provincial Government and reportedly resigned from the Department yesterday and left for Shanghai to take office.

Local News

The Municipal Executive Committee requests an investigation into Zhang Shouyong, President of Guangda University, and requests the reinstatement of Yang Shuchun's student status 94

The National Society reported that Yang Shuchun, a student who was unjustly expelled from Guanghua University during the recent student unrest, had previously had his student status reinstated by the Municipal Executive Committee's referral to the school, as reported in the previous newspaper. It is now reported that Zhang Shouyong, the president of the university, replied to the Municipal Executive Committee yesterday, stating that Yang Shuchun's reinstatement could not be processed and that a transfer certificate should be issued and processed by the registrar's office. After receiving the letter, the Municipal Executive Committee resolved at its eighty-first regular meeting to request the Central Government to order Guanghua University to reinstate Yang Shuchun's student status and to request the Central Government to investigate the president of the university.

Municipal Education Bureau's Instructions on Yafeng Elementary School 95

The founder is urged to register the school, but the bureau has no record of the case.

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Instruction No. 15, Shanghai Private Yafeng Elementary School founder Zhu Xinglin, "Received your report. Since the report does not specify the date of submission of the registration form and there is no school address, this bureau has no record of the case. Your request will not be discussed and you are hereby notified." Xu Peihuang, Director, January 23, 20th year of the Republic of China.

Four to One Victory Over Santo Tomas

Tomorrow's Third Interport Soccer Trial Match 99

3 PM at Shen Garden

丨Tomorrow's Westerners Association Schedule丨

Last Night's Basketball Game: Northeast Defeats Labor University Again 100

Thirty-Six to Nineteen

Labor University Performs Admirably Despite Defeat

Northeast University Wins Fourth Time

Tomorrow Night at 7 PM: Battle with Zhonggong

The Northeastern University basketball team, which has been winning consecutively, met Labor University at the Chinese Basketball Hall last night. The result was a score of thirty-six to nineteen, marking the fourth victory for Northeastern University since arriving in Shanghai. Labor University put up fierce resistance in the first half, with Northeastern University only winning by two points, earning them a lot of applause. Unfortunately, Labor University's stamina faltered later, leading to their defeat. The referee was Shu Hong.

Never Relax, Labor University is Formidable 101

The performance of both teams in the first half of last night's game was extremely exciting. Labor University's skills have improved significantly. Although Northeastern University is strong, they could not find a way to beat Labor University. The score fluctuated constantly, and there were several ties. Labor University closely guarded Northeastern University's forward, Yuan Tingrui, making it difficult for him to move, which was unexpected. At the sound of the referee's whistle, the two teams collided and ran back and forth, holding each other to a draw several times. Yuan Tingrui's long shot finally broke the deadlock, but Labor University's Song Jinhai also scored one point due to Zhao Zhizhi's foul. Yuan Tingrui scored again, giving Northeastern University a 5-1 lead. However, Labor University, with excellent coordination, tied the score. Northeastern University scored again, and Labor University also scored, bringing the score to seven-seven and nine-nine, with no winner in sight. The entire stadium was tense. Labor University unexpectedly scored, taking the lead with 11-9.

Changing Tactics, Northeast University Finds a Turning Point 102

Finding no progress, Northeast University called for a timeout and changed their tactics. They realized that rushing too quickly would inevitably lead to chaos, and Yuan Tingrui's movements were restricted due to the close marking, making it necessary to change their strategy. They proceeded cautiously, avoiding reckless shots and instead adjusting their defenders to attack. Sure enough, Ma Bingjun broke free, tying the score at 11-11. Once this tactic was successful, they tried again and scored again. In the first half, Northeastern University won over Labor University by two points, with a score of 13-11.

Take it Slow, Northeast University Wins Again 103

Knowing that a fierce attack would be futile and even detrimental, Northeastern University maintained the previous strategy from the beginning of the second half, with the defenders moving forward and Yuan Tingrui taking the opportunity to attack. Northeastern University won one victory after another, and Labor University was trapped by their strategy, falling behind by 11-25. From then on, they were severely demoralized and unable to recover.

Stamina Declines, Labor University Loses 104

Labor University's strength in the first half followed by weakness in the second half was mainly due to a lack of stamina. The close marking was also less effective in the second half than in the first half, and with the change in the situation, panic appeared. They became increasingly anxious when attacking, resulting in many missed opportunities, which was a pity. Looking back at the first half, one cannot help but feel a sense of regret over the difference in strength. The final score was 36-19, with Northeastern University winning.

The situation of the Jinan soccer team's expedition to the Philippines, which is famous at home and abroad, has already been recorded in our newspaper's previous dispatch. La Salle's Achievements in the Philippines 106

La Salle Athletic Club is also known throughout the Philippines for its strong combat power. The team's players have three years of experience in cooperation. The players are all alumni of the school, forming an elite organization, and two of them have attended the Far Eastern Games (one is the Iron General guarding the door). The team won the first place in the 1930 Manila Athletic Association's Group A championship. In September of last year, they joined the soccer association organized by the Spanish sports community in the city, and as a result, they tied for first place with another soccer team. They also won second place in the All-Philippine University Soccer Tournament last year. The team's historical record is enough to be proud of. This match is no ordinary match, and they have also enlisted their former alumnus, the current captain of the Spanish soccer team, Minzhisu Na, as the right guard, to consolidate their strength. They also intend to compete with the Jinan team to determine who is superior.

Valiant Athletes Take to the Field 107

The venue was in the Carnival soccer stadium. The turnout for this event was huge, especially among the overseas Chinese. By 3 o'clock, the area outside the stadium was crowded with traffic. The prime seats, valued at one dollar, were all taken by 4 o'clock, and spectators were still surging in to buy tickets, reminiscent of the old Lehua scene. It is estimated that there were more than 3,000 spectators, with overseas Chinese accounting for seven or eight tenths (foreigners usually don't finish work until 5 o'clock), which shows their enthusiasm for supporting Jinan. Then, the athletes from both teams took to the field. The Jinan team members wore blue shirts, white pants, and orange-black striped socks, looking valiant and spirited as they took the field. The members of both teams also wore a white-green color scheme, showing their bravery. At half past four, the judges tossed a coin to choose the goal, and the captains of both teams presented flowers to each other and shook hands to show respect. Then, Lu Se, a local enthusiast of sports, performed the opening ceremony, and with the sound of the silver whistle, the battle began.

Two Teams Compete, Displaying Divine Power 108

The ball was kicked by Lucesus towards the Jianan left inside forward. The opposing team, taking advantage of the situation, pressed in with the ball. Halfway there, it was intercepted by our center half, Zhuang Shihong, who passed it to the right wing, Mei Hongbao. Mei then advanced along the sideline, but was entangled by the opposing left back. All the opposing forwards arrived, but fortunately, our center back defended effectively, preventing them from capitalizing. Soon after, Dai Linjing took a shot straight at the goal, but it was stubbornly resisted by the opposing right back, who then launched a counter-attack. Fortunately, Chen Zhenhe, Feng Yunyou, and Jiang Shanjing bravely defended, preventing defeat. This was the situation in the first ten minutes of the match. Later, Mei Hongbao received a pass from Dai Linjing and struck with all his might. The audience applauded loudly, expecting the ball to rush straight into the goal, but it missed by just over five inches, hitting the crossbar. They missed the opportunity to score first, much to the regret of the audience.

Penalty Kick Scores a Goal 109

After our team missed the opportunity to score, the opposing team became very active. The right forward received a pass from the back and dribbled straight in, shooting from seven or eight yards outside the goal. Liang Guanlian had not yet recovered from his illness, feeling heavy-headed and unsteady on his feet, unable to make the save. This allowed the opposing team to open the scoring. The Westerners cheered wildly, but fortunately there were not many of them, so their momentum was not overwhelming. Soon, the opposing team surged again, and the right wing kicked in another goal. The force of the attack was truly unexpected by the audience. At this time, our team realized that the opponents were not to be taken lightly, so they rallied their spirits and changed their strategy. Chen Zhenhe was positioned as the center back, running and supporting all areas. They tried to shoot at the opponent's goal several times, but all were blocked by the opposing goalkeeper. For example, Dai Linjing displayed his long-range shooting skills, aiming directly at the goal, but it was saved and rebounded by the goalkeeper. As our team pressed into the opposing territory, the opposing team forcefully collided with our players, resulting in a penalty kick. Chen Zhenhe kicked it in, and our team finally opened the scoring. At this time, the overseas Chinese who were worried about the Jianan team showed a slight smile, hoping that they could take advantage of this momentum and turn defeat into victory. However, the opposing team worked even harder to charge at our goal, and the opposing right forward scored another goal from the left. The first half ended with a score of one to three, which was a great surprise to our overseas Chinese compatriots.

Changing Formation, Morale Greatly Boosted 110

The whistle blew again, and the teams reorganized to continue the match. On our team, the right center back on the central defensive line was replaced by Shutang. Chen Zhenhe remained as the center back, and Zhuang Shihong played as the left center back. Each player displayed great power, and the formation showed great improvement. Our players tirelessly ran around the opponent's goal, but it was as if one man was guarding the gate, like a mud seal on Hangu Pass, and they could not find a way in. Fortunately, the opposing team committed another foul, resulting in a free kick. Dai Linjing took the kick, and the ball went diagonally into the right corner, scoring directly.

Jinan Football Team's Dai Linjing (left) and LaSalle Team Captain Cuxishou (right) shake hands and exchange flowers before the start of the match.
