Warning to the Corporation: The Shanghai Great World Savings Department Daily and Night Bank Creditors' Committee issued a letter warning the board of directors of the Gongfa Corporation, stating, "The Great World Amusement Park Savings Department and the Shanghai Daily and Night Bank, which belong to your corporation, suddenly announced the suspension of deposit payments on the 20th of this month and appointed personnel for liquidation, causing countless creditors to feel shaken. According to the resolution of this creditors' committee, we urge your corporation to pay off the principal and interest of all depositors of the two departments by February 7th of this year to demonstrate credibility and safeguard the creditors' rights. We hereby notify you. This is addressed to the board of directors of the Shanghai Gongfa Corporation."

Declaration Published: Following the death of Mr. Huang Chujiu, his relatives and friends organized a post-mortem committee. The committee decided to maintain the normal operation of Huang's businesses, such as the Jiufu, Fuchang, Zhongxi, and Zhongfa companies. However, the Great World Savings Department and the Daily and Night Bank suspended deposit payments and announced liquidation, causing the rights of the creditors of these two departments to be shaken. During Mr. Huang's lifetime, he relied on these two institutions to absorb the hard-earned money of countless ordinary people, using it as a foundation for developing other businesses. Therefore, the depositors of these two departments contributed greatly to Mr. Huang's various enterprises. In terms of both reason and morality, the creditors of these two departments should enjoy priority and special protection without any doubt. Now, the opposite is happening, which is unreasonable and unfair. Furthermore, according to the principles of bankruptcy law in various countries, creditors of savings departments must be repaid first, which is a worldwide practice. This is done to protect the interests of poor depositors and to consolidate the credibility of the savings industry. Moreover, the creditors of these two departments are mostly poor households, with deposits ranging from thousands or hundreds to tens or even a few yuan. This is their hard-earned money accumulated through daily labor and frugality. Once it is shaken, there is a risk to their lives and property. Just look at the weeping elderly women and men in front of the two institutions every day, the shop assistants and laborers beating their chests and stamping their feet on the road. The situation is unspeakably tragic. If the principal and interest are not maintained and repaid first, there will inevitably be life-threatening actions during this cold winter season, or even desperation, leading to major incidents, which would not be fortunate for either side. We earnestly hope that all sectors will uphold justice and provide assistance so that the hard-earned money of thousands

Page 16

of households can be preserved. This is of great importance and extremely urgent.

Dong Jiangshi Urges Trial for Divorce Case 184

Submits Document to the French Concession Court Yesterday

Xinsheng Society: The case of lawyer Dong Yu suing his wife Jiang Youzhi for suffering from lung disease and requesting a divorce has been reported in detail in this newspaper. After the French Concession Court heard the case, it ordered a trial reconciliation. However, due to the complexity of the matter, it ultimately failed. Now, his wife, Jiang, believes that the case has been pending for too long and that complications have arisen. She has now hired two lawyers, Sheng Shenghiu and Wang Kanghou, to file a petition with the French Concession Court, requesting a trial. The original petition is as follows: "For the matter of falsely accusing lung disease and filing for divorce, the case has been pending for too long, and we have repeatedly requested a trial. The defendant, Jiang, was sued for divorce by the plaintiff, Dong Yu, also known as Dong Jingxi, in November of last year, who claimed that she had long suffered from lung disease. The judge ordered reconciliation twice. However, the plaintiff had no intention of reconciliation. The defendant submitted a petition and the Women's Association also sent letters requesting a trial. Since the beginning of the year, almost a month has passed. However, the plaintiff has come up with strange ideas, hiring two female teachers in the name of teaching his six-year-old son. One of them is lodging in the pavilion room where the defendant lives, and the other, dressed extravagantly like a noble lady, comes to the house in the evening and leaves late at night. The plaintiff has contracted the disease as a result of this and has also hired a couple who were previously unacquainted to take care of him on his sickbed. All of these situations have been witnessed by servants. How can there be any family order left? It is thought that if this case is suspended for a long time, not only will the defendant's status never be clarified, but living with relatives is also not a long-term solution, and it is even more difficult to prevent other changes from occurring, leading to abuse in her remaining life. The only hope is to rely on the sanctity of the law for protection. Therefore, we humbly request the judge to set a date to summon both parties for trial and make a judgment in accordance with the law. This would be a great kindness."

Report on Water Meter Damage Due to Freezing – Water Company Repairs Without Charge 185

Due to the severe cold weather in recent days, water meters in many households in the city have been damaged due to freezing. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has heard that users are complaining because they believe that water meter freezing is a matter of weather, but the water company will still demand compensation according to regulations; otherwise, they will not repair it or will even stop supplying water, hindering the economic life of the public. Therefore, on the 20th of this month, the bureau separately convened the business directors of the inland and Zhabei water companies to the bureau for discussion. Although the regulations of the companies stipulate that the user is responsible for any damage to the water pipes and all accessories within the water meter, there are no clear regulations on who is responsible for the damage caused by water meter freezing. It was agreed that when users discover a water source interruption or water meter freezing, they should immediately report it to the company. The company will send workers to repair or replace it and restore the water supply immediately without charging any fees. If the user does not report to the company at the time and repairs it without authorization, resulting in damage to the water meter, and then reports to the company for repair, the company may repair it first and restore the water supply, but all damage and repair costs should be compensated by the user. This method is fair to both users and the company. It is heard that the bureau has ordered the two companies to comply and notify all users to follow the regulations.

Headquarters Sends Personnel to Shanghai to Investigate the Nie Dianbang Case 186

Question of Whether Nie Dianbang Was the Mastermind

Trial Can Only Begin After Evidence Is Complete

Nie Dianbang, the murderer who assassinated the revolutionary martyr Chen Yingshi, was arrested in Shanghai at the beginning of the month and detained by the Public Security Bureau. Later, following an order from President Chiang Kai-shek of the National Government, the suspect was transferred to Nanjing for trial. It was done on the 13th of the month. Now it is learned that President Chiang believes that the case is of great importance and cannot be handled hastily. Guilt cannot be determined without a detailed investigation, so he has sent personnel to Shanghai to conduct an investigation. The personnel came to Shanghai yesterday to conduct the investigation, and everything is being kept secret for the time being. However, according to the personnel, the assassination of Chen Yingshi was far back in the fifth year of the Republic, fifteen years ago. The mastermind, Yuan Shikai, is undoubtedly guilty. As for whether Nie Dianbang was the murderer in the case, it cannot be determined without a detailed investigation. It is planned to investigate the lawyer who handled the case, the confessions of the suspects obtained after the case occurred, and the fingerprints at the time. After the evidence has been gathered, headquarters can begin the trial.

Public Works Department to Hire Two Types of Trainees 187

Health Inspectors and Fire Brigade Officers

The Public Works Department of the Public Concession will hire eight Chinese trainees to train them for future appointments as health inspectors in the Health Department. It will also hire another ten Chinese trainees to train them for future appointments as fire brigade officers in the Fire Department. Applicants must be proficient in English and the Shanghai dialect, as well as Mandarin, and be able to write applicable documents in English and Chinese. The age requirement is between twenty-one and twenty-five years old. The first year will be a probationary trainee with a monthly salary of seventy-five yuan. From the second year onwards, the monthly salary will be one hundred yuan. The training period for health trainees is approximately six and a half years, and the training period for fire trainees is three years. After passing each exam, the salary will be increased by fifteen yuan. After completing the training period, they will be appointed as junior staff with a monthly salary starting from two hundred and fifty yuan and increasing by grade.

Wang Hanlun's Appeal Case Against the Great Southeast Company Settled 191

Movie star Wang Hanlun, previously noticed that the Great Southeast Tobacco Company of this city had, without her consent, used her name and image to manufacture "Wang Hanlun" brand cigarettes, which were sold in areas such as Hebei and Tianjin. Believing this to be a deliberate infringement of her rights to her name and image, she entrusted a lawyer to file a lawsuit against the Great Southeast Company with the Shanghai French Concession Court, seeking compensation for damage to her reputation and an end to the infringement. The first instance judgment found that the cigarettes in question were produced by the Jianhua Tobacco Company and that the lawsuit should have been filed against Jianhua. The lawsuit against the Great Southeast Company was dismissed due to the wrong party being sued. Dissatisfied with the judgment, Ms. Wang engaged lawyer Dong Chi to file an appeal according to the law. The appeal detailed the errors in the original judgment. Upon learning of the appeal, the Great Southeast Company had someone approach Ms. Wang to seek a settlement. After several negotiations, Ms. Wang agreed. A formal settlement agreement was signed on January 17th. The main terms of the settlement were: (1) The Great Southeast Company would compensate Ms. Wang for losses and legal fees, totaling four thousand yuan. (2) The company would immediately cease the production and sale of "Wang Hanlun" brand cigarettes, and any existing stock would be destroyed. If the company continued to produce and sell the cigarettes in the future, Ms. Wang would have the right to seek an end to the infringement and receive appropriate compensation. (3) The plaintiff would immediately submit a statement to the French Concession Court to withdraw the appeal, demonstrating a determination to settle the dispute.

Feng Residence Wedding Route for Vehicles 192

Enter from Nanjing Road... Exit from Jiujiang Road

On the 26th of this month, Feng Bingnan, a businessman from Feng, will hold a wedding ceremony for his eldest son, Zhenduo. The ceremony will be held at the Great Eastern Hotel on Yinhua Street, Nanjing Road. The Shanghai Municipal Council Police Department, anticipating a large number of vehicles due to the wedding guests, has decided to arrange the traffic flow on Yinhua Street as follows: From 8:00 AM to 2:00 PM and from 6:00 PM to 12:00 AM on that day, all vehicles going to Yinhua Street, whether coming from the west or the east, should enter from Nanjing Road. Those wishing to enter from Jiujiang Road must detour to Nanjing Road and enter Yinhua Street from there. The north side of Yinhua Street will be used as the entrance, and the south side as the exit, to avoid congestion.

Further Report on the Baohe Jewelry Store Robbery Case Solved 193

Fu Guoxi and others confess without denial.

Another suspect, Wang A'da, was arrested yesterday.

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, detectives Su Sheng, Wang Shifu, Lü Xingchun, Chen Jiren, and others from the Detective Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau solved the robbery case of the Lao Baohe Jewelry Store at the intersection of Zhongshan Road and Datong Road in Zhabei. The criminals Fu Guoxi, Huang Dianchen (also known as "Little Pig Head"), and Zhang Yangzhi were arrested, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. Captain Lu believes that, given the series of robbery cases during the winter prevention period, strict interrogation of the arrested criminals is necessary to deter others. The team ordered the foreman to strictly apprehend the remaining suspects and brought Fu Guoxi to No. 124 Jiaotong Road, where Wang A'da was arrested. The confessions of the criminals are summarized below:

Fu Guoxi (also known as Fu Xiaoxizi) confessed: 29 years old, from Funing, works as a vegetable farmer. At 10:00 AM today, Zheng San, Huang Dianchen, Zhang Yangzhi, and I went to Xibaoxing Road and identified a cloth store. At 5:00 PM, Huang Dianchen and I took a loaded pistol to the store to rob it. We were arrested at Pingjiang Bridge. I, Zheng San, Huang Dianchen, Zhang Yangzhi, Xiao Bazi, Li Sangenbao, and others also robbed the jewelry store on the east side of the Zhabei Dayang Bridge. We stole over one hundred yuan, 34 catties of silverware, and a sheepskin robe. We divided the loot in an open space behind the Jianghuai Public Hall. I received 18 yuan and over six catties of silverware. Huang Dianchen (also known as "Little Pig Head") confessed: 24 years old, from Funing, works as a rickshaw puller. Today at 4:00 PM, Fu Xiaoxizi and I went to the Xibaoxing Road vegetable market to rob a cloth store and handed me a loaded pistol. I, Fu, and several strangers, a total of seven people, robbed the jewelry store on the east side of the Dayang Bridge and obtained 12 yuan and a bag of loose silver, which Fu Xiaoxizi exchanged. Zhang Yangzhi confessed: 30 years old, from Funing, works as a rickshaw puller. I know Zheng San and Huang Dianchen. Huang and others invited me to stay at their house and advised me to sell candy instead of pulling a rickshaw, saying that pulling a rickshaw was too hard. I replied that I had no capital. They said they would go out with me the next day and help me. They said I could stand guard outside. In the afternoon, Zheng San and others invited me to Fu Xiaoxizi's house in Zhujiamiao, Zhabei, and we went to Baohe Jewelry Store on the east side of Dayang Bridge (Zhongshan Road) to rob it. We found it was closed, so we dug a hole in the wall of a newly built house next door. Zheng San first entered, followed by Fu Xiaoxizi and three strangers. Ji San and I stood guard outside. I received ten yuan in stolen goods. At 5:00 PM on the 22nd afternoon, Zheng San came to my house again and called me, Fu Xiaoxizi, and Little Pig Head to take two pistols and go to Xibaoxing Road to rob a cloth store. We were inspected and arrested at the Shuimuting Bridge. Zheng San escaped immediately. Another suspect, Wang A'da, was apprehended, and is currently under strict interrogation.

Meihua Dance Troupe Returns to Shanghai 194

To Perform at the Central Grand Theater

The entire 40-member Meihua Dance Troupe performed at the Hangzhou Movie Theater for six days from the 15th to the 20th, with every performance filled to more than 100% capacity. The troupe returned to Shanghai on the 21st and will rest for ten days. From the 31st to January 2nd, they will perform a dance show with ten items at the Central Grand Theater. In addition to the sensational "Seven Emotions" (which has been recorded as a record at the request of Mr. Pan Jiarui, manager of the Victory Record Company), they will also perform a newly choreographed and first-time performance of the grand and sorrowful dance drama "Unseen Last Year's People." The drama depicts the suffering of war in great depth, with lyrics containing sorrowful feelings in over ten stanzas. The harmony of the musical accompaniment is also exceptional.

Candle Industry Association Refuses Workers' Wage Increase 195

The Shanghai Candle Industry Association held a general meeting yesterday to discuss the request for a wage increase from the workers. Representatives were invited to attend mediation. A total of 38 members attended, and Tong Guanwen was elected as the chairman. After the opening ceremony, the following motions were proposed: (1) A request from the Social Affairs Bureau to send two representatives to attend mediation for the Candle Industry Union's wage increase request. It was decided to appoint Shen Yuzhang and Mi Qinrui as the fully authorized representatives. (2) How should the Association respond to the Candle Industry Union's wage increase request during the mediation? It was decided to firmly reject the request based on the resolution passed at the general meeting on November 3rd of the previous year, stating the reasons. (3) Should the Association's announcement prohibiting the gifting of candles be published in the "Republic Daily"? It was decided to publish it on the front page for three days. After discussing other motions, all were passed and the meeting adjourned.

Dechang Lace Sells Well Domestically and Internationally 196

Lace is a famous specialty of our country. Mr. Wang Xiangfu, a major businessman, has been studying this industry for over a decade and founded the Dechang Lace Company. They produce fine lace handkerchiefs, tea towels, tablecloths, women's shawls, curtains, and more, offering a wide variety of products. The materials are exquisite, and the production is excellent. The products sell well both domestically and internationally in large quantities. The company is large-scale with numerous products, resulting in unusually low prices. The designs are too numerous to list. The distribution location is No. 248 Rue du Père Huc, Shanghai, telephone number 71082.

Deyu Factory Releases New "Coin" Brand Flashlight 197

The Deyu Tongji Electric Factory, which previously produced the "Horse" brand flashlight, known for its excellent manufacturing and sales in various ports, is well-received by all sectors. It is now reported that the factory is continuing to release a second product, named the "Coin" brand. Although the price is slightly lower than the "Horse" brand, the manufacturing and quality are the same. Made entirely of copper coins, it is exceptionally exquisite. In recent days, merchants from other ports have already heard the news and placed orders.

National Products Market Holds Large-Scale Cotton Textile Sale 198

The China National Products United Market, to promote national goods, unite manufacturers, expand sales, and resist foreign economic aggression, will hold a large-scale cotton textile sale and promotion event starting today. At the same time, new dramas, comic skits, and other entertainment will be provided to add to the enjoyment. It is said that to show appreciation to customers, anyone who purchases over one yuan in the self-operated business department of the market will receive a beautiful picture and tickets as gifts. At this time of high gold prices and low silver prices, it is a good opportunity for Chinese people to use national goods. When the time comes, ladies and gentlemen will flock to the market to purchase national goods, creating a grand scene.

Police officer Wang Wenqing of the No. 2584 Old Lapel Badge from the Caojiadu Sixth District Police Station in western Shanghai lost a police badge a few days ago. In addition to reporting it to the Public Security Bureau, it is hereby declared void.

Quanchang Shop Hires New Technician 200

Quanchang Shop on Rue Édouard VII, Sanyange Bridge, specializes in real gold jewelry, pearls, diamonds, glasses, etc. A new technician from Broadway has been hired to set novel jewelry and various unusual brooches, kerosene diamonds, etc. Glasses are fitted for one yuan per pair, with eye exams and light tests provided free of charge, so ladies in Shanghai are all vying to be first, it is said.

Director Qian's Leather Briefcase Recovered 201

Qian Shouheng, director of the First Branch of the Second District, lost a leather briefcase on the evening of the 20th of this month, containing staff certificates, party certificates, inspection certificates, and silver yuan. He immediately requested reissuance from the higher-level agencies. However, the briefcase was picked up by a legitimate merchant on Min'guo Road that night, who immediately returned it to Director Qian. Qian praised him greatly and rewarded him with five yuan for transportation expenses. The person thanked him and left.

Weather Report 202

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The weather is clear and cold. There is fog in the Yangtze River basin. The coastal areas of the country have normal winter seasonal winds. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 50.7 degrees, and the lowest was 35.4 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 40.8 degrees, and the lowest was 30.4 degrees.

Art World

New Efforts 203

— Wang Daoyuan

Last time our school held an exhibition, it actually gained the attention of the general public, which made us very happy. We already know that the public's demand for art and the passion for art have not diminished. The public's attitude towards our efforts has not been unconscious, nor has it been met with scorn and ridicule. This alone is enough for us to put down our heavy brushes and feel quite relieved. What's more, there are art lovers who have given us kind words of encouragement and endless motivation. In addition to expressing our gratitude, we can only hold on to our future and work even harder to exchange our entire energy for the extremely bright future of art. This is our current ambition, which depends on the efforts of our entire art community.

Since returning to China, I have been buried in Jiangwan Road, spending all day with students and colors. Since deciding to build our own school building, my mind has been filled with things like wood, bricks, and tiles, and I seem to be busy enough. I have never said a word about the domestic art scene and my own work. Now that I have picked up my pen, I have to say something.

Everything from last year has become the past. In this new year, we should naturally make some new efforts. The object of our current demands, ostentation and embellishment, seems to have lost its authority. What we hope for is a great soul that melts us in a painting. However, where the brush should stop and where the mind should lift its head are not easy decisions in painting. In short, a painting with a sublime and rich thought, no matter how rough and ugly it is, will always be more valuable than a delicate and skillful work that lacks content. Therefore, John Ruskin has this to say: The best article and the best picture should be declared in all the things that can be moved and decorated on the dignity contained within it, but when it reaches the most excellent state, these things are still useless... We prefer the simple words and lines that can trigger an idea in its original beautiful state.

Now we know that the life of a painter lies in the internal majesty of his work, and external exquisite gorgeousness is not the goal we are pursuing. At the same time, we should clarify our minds and find our painting materials from the contradictory background of the current society.

The era has come to us. We should firmly grasp our brushes and make the "force" of art the vanguard of the era. Our painters, our "force"!

Speaking of our school, the Shanghai Art College, at this moment, can be regarded as an art group that is fighting with the times. Although it has only one year of history, its efforts over the past year have been presented to the public, and it is unwilling to boast too much about itself. Its future situation can only be expressed through its own actual work. Actual work is its content. We don't need much exaggeration and external decoration. We especially want to smash the kind of unchanging so-called academic style of regressive traditional forces.

It is worth mentioning that this year, our school has a social art service to create a strong artistic atmosphere, which must start from this effort. The first of these efforts must start from the painting education of children. We firmly believe that:

With such a decision, our neighboring elementary schools will be voluntarily receiving their art education from us, giving full interest to the drawing courses that have always been neglected, so that the boundless children's minds can be clearly expressed, and the small and skillful hands can be reflected in nature. What a divine and wonderful thing! The creation of an artistic children's world, what a great success for the art world!

Let's look at our neighboring country, Japanese painters. Since advocating the free painting movement for children, what satisfactory results have they obtained? They shouted loudly there,

"We aim to make our art the most trend-following thing, and feel that this thing must start from the painting education of children." With this, the impact was great, and all places gave sympathy and support, so a lively new scene appeared in Japanese art education.

Now we should not be behind others and do the same.

Indeed, "beauty" is such a thing that implies the secrets of nature and inspires profound wisdom. If you rely solely on the imitation of models or the teaching of masters, then "beauty" will ultimately degenerate.

Needless to say, the drawing class hours in elementary schools in our country are considered not very important subjects. How the results are, the school does not pay much attention to it, as if it is a dispensable thing, but it is only brought to decorate it. The teachers mostly give them a model to copy and perfunctorily spend one or two hours, so the children also feel bored. Now the most important thing for us is to abolish the copybooks and let the children express themselves directly. We firmly believe that the shapes and colors that children directly absorb from "nature" must be more interesting than copying the crude printed adult paintings.

Fundamentally, in children's painting, the perception and feeling are different from those of adults. Children have their own observations and emotions. The professor can only explain it to enlighten them, and must not let them blindly follow the works of the model. What is especially important is to make the children hold a kind of power, so that the children can freely describe the object and fully exert their own perceptions, which is to make him expand his own power towards nature.

Copybooks are a withered and lifeless thing. The hearts and hands of children are full of vitality. It is such a boring thing to bind lively hearts and hands with a withered tool.

Here we know that that kind of imitative copying can only create an immutable inferior nature of imitation in children, and the immeasurable creativity is suppressed.

However, the country is flooded, and almost all elementary schools are doing copybook life, and the so-called educators do not care about the lack of progress in art education. As for the training of painting, how important a relationship it has with the cultivation of "beauty" for children, they have never dreamed of. This is very bleak for the future of art education.

Now we are determined to work hard in this area, and hope that enthusiastic educators will teach me.

Talking about the First Exhibition of the Japanese Independent Art Association 204

— Lin Yong

The Japanese Independent Art Association was formed by seceding from the Nikakai. I said last year that the first exhibition opened on January 11, 1931. Independent art, in Japan, is indeed independent. I dare say that in the Japanese art world, although it is not as successful as the Nikakai, the art group, in addition to the Nikakai, is the Independent Art Association, which started following 1930, that can be hoped to resist the Imperial Art Academy. Even in the works of this first exhibition, we can clearly see the aspirations of their members. Of course, many people who saw it said that all the works selected by the newcomers were not worth seeing. This is the truth, but this is just a one-sided attack. But the efforts of the members' responsibilities are indeed efforts, and some writers' works have made more progress than before.

The works in the entire venue are all post-impressionist, Fauvist groups, using yellow, green, red, and black as the main silver colors. The brushstrokes are impulsive, the screens are symbolic, and the objects are only used as the outlines of their screens. Such works in Japan, even in the Eastern art world, do have the possibility of independence.

The selected works are mostly encouraging new entrants to promote the new Fauvist group, I think.

Tanaka Kinuyo is the first actress whose work was selected for a Japanese art exhibition. This is not a strange thing in the atmosphere of emerging art. Now the era is new, and art is the guide of the new era. They have such a declaration,

"Art needs the support of the public, and the established art world, at first, did not pay attention to the works of female writers. If you only take a look at it, it is also good."

Mr. Katsuzo Satomi said, "The bell does not ring, the masses will not leave. Has that bell been heard?"

Mr. Shigeyoshi Hayashi said, "Fresh works are pleasant, and the tendency is definitely biased towards the New Fauvism. There are various colors, but the avoidance of different colors is done in this way. There are many female works selected."

The works of realism and naturalism from the past can be seen to be broken. The rules of qualifications have all been destroyed. When we step into their venue, we will know very clearly with our eyes, strange postures, stimulating screens, irregular lines, licentious colors, mechanical beauty expression, and scientific depiction. We will definitely be surprised when we see it. Mr. Zenzo Kojima's "Independent Art Debut" screen is five nude women, and the one in the middle is the symbol of independent art. The two next to them are independent art writers, one wearing clothes for them and one wearing decorations for them, making them beautiful, making them magnificent, and making them charming. The purple background, we can naturally feel is noble, and the bright eyes lead the footsteps to find the road to light. The other works all have very pleasant brushstrokes, simple colors, and uncomplicated compositions, which are well worth our appreciation.

The scientific and mechanical description of Ichiro Fukuzawa is the most obvious. Whether the screen or the title of the painting is a mysterious comedy, satirizing the world, and comparing life.

Rouault is the most famous of modern New Fauvism. Many of the works in this independent art exhibition are similar to his, with unlined brushstrokes and crazy tones, expressing the most beautiful ugliness of the world. The works of Katsuzo Satomi are so similar. Mr. Satomi can be regarded as the Eastern Rouault.

The works of Kigaigawa have poetic sentiment, three-dimensional lines, a quiet yet frantic tone, and irregular outlines, which will truly make us tremble in silence when we see them.

The works of Takeshi Hayashi were initially an allusion to Matisse, but now they have gone to the outline of Matisse. The colors are very clearly distinguished from them.

There are also other works by Shigeyoshi Hayashi, Yasunori Suzuki, Shiro Takada, Afu Suzuki, etc., which are all very noteworthy. They are all pioneers of the new Fauvist group in Japan.

In the Independent Art Exhibition, 271 works were selected from 3,751 works for us to appreciate. It can be understood that this number is not indiscriminate selection.

Their efforts are indeed worthy of being imitated by the art world in our country. It is heard that the domestic art world is not silent, but silent as if dead. This is certainly because the level of art of the Chinese people is too shallow and they despise art too much. But on the other hand, it is that the art world is too irresponsible, which cannot be escaped.

I hope that the Chinese people will at least imitate people's efforts.
